<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наоборот.html>наоборо́т</a> (1181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оборот.html>оборо́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oborót</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наоборот.html>наоборо́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naoborót</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>inside out, back to front</li>
<li>vice versa, the other way round, conversely</li>
<li>on the contrary, to the contrary</li></ol>

***наотрез.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наотрез.html>наотре́з</a> (12365)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отрез.html>отре́з</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">otréz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, known since the 18th century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наотрез.html>наотре́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naotréz</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>firmly, definitely
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отказать.html>отказа́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наотрез.html>наотре́з</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otkazátʹ <b>naotréz</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to refuse</b> flatly</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***нападать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нападать.html>напада́ть</a> (5175)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нападать.html>напада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to attack, to fall on, to assault, to descend <i>(on)</i></li>
<li>to come across, to come upon, to hit on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja napál na myslʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the thought occurred me</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(feeling, condition)</i> to come <i>(over)</i>, to grip, to seize, to overcome</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нападение.html>нападе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">napadénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́сть</a> (7770)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napástʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́сти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́сти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́стей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>misfortune, bad luck, trouble</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napástʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нападать.html>напада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to attack, to fall on, to assault, to descend <i>(on)</i></li>
<li>to come across, to come upon, to hit on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:напасть.html>напа́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja <b>napál</b> na myslʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the thought occurred to me</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(feeling, condition)</i> to come <i>(over)</i>, to grip, to seize, to overcome</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напевать.html>напева́ть</a> (7678)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напеть.html>напе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">napétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напевать.html>напева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напеть.html>напе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hum <i>(a melody)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sing <i>(demonstrating a melody)</i></li>
<li>to have one's singing recorded <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:напевать.html>напева́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:диск.html>диск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>napevátʹ</b> disk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to record a disk (of one's singing)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slander</li></ol>

***напеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напеть.html>напе́ть</a> (30908)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:петь.html>пе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напеть.html>напе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напевать.html>напева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hum <i>(a melody)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sing <i>(demonstrating a melody)</i></li>
<li>to have one's singing recorded <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:напеть.html>напе́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:диск.html>диск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>napétʹ</b> disk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to record a disk (of one's singing)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to slander</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печатать.html>печа́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pečátatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***напечь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:напечь.html>напе́чь</a> (26710)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>печь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напечь.html>напе́чь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napéčʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to bake <i>(certain quantity)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:напечь.html>напекла́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тарелка.html>таре́лку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:блинчик.html>бли́нчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná <b>napeklá</b> tarélku blínčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">she made a plateful of pancakes</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heat by the sun
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:напечь.html>напекло́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голову</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>napekló</b> golovu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">my head aches from staying in the sun too long</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***напильник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>напильник</a> (23142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Apparently from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">напили́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">napilítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but the verb "to file" is actually <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">опили́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">opilítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>напи́льник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">napílʹnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напильник.html>напи́льника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напильник.html>напи́льники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напильник.html>напи́льников</a></b>)
</p>
